How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

Loot Chart

#1

- Gear: Pants
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: Legs
- Color: Green
- Stat Buffs
    - Movement Speed ✦ = Lx2
    - Energy Generation = 2
    - Initiative = L÷2
    - Range ✦ = Lx1.25
- Actives:
    - [Here! A Gift!](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Here!+A+Gift!)
    - [Healing Touch](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Healing+Touch)
    - You have access to Tiers I-III of each of your Actives.
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500
- Aesthetic: Pbosh (Viking/Heavy, Rough Metal)
